# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="e8ea2-102">Types obsolètes dans le .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e8ea2-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="e8ea2-103"><a name="introduction"></a> Les tableaux de cet article, organisés par assembly, répertorient les types qui sont obsolètes dans le [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] et le [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e8ea2-103"><a name="introduction"></a> The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e8ea2-104">Utilisez les liens suivants pour consulter la liste des types obsolètes et des alternatives recommandées dans chaque assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e8ea2-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e8ea2-105">Ces types étant obsolètes, tous leurs membres le sont également.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e8ea2-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e8ea2-106">Pour obtenir la liste des membres obsolètes supplémentaires dans la bibliothèque de classes .NET Framework, consultez [Membres obsolètes](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e8ea2-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="e8ea2-928">Assembly : IEHost.dll et IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e8ea2-928">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>
